    protein_name VARCHAR(50),
    gene_id INT REFERENCES gene_info(gene_id),
    length INT,
    sequence TEXT
);

CREATE TABLE gene_info (
    gene_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    gene_name VARCHAR(50),
    chromosome VARCHAR(10),
    start_position INT,
    end_position INT
);

CREATE TABLE mutation_info (
    mutation_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    gene_id INT REFERENCES gene_info(gene_id),
    mutation_description TEXT
);</t><stat>INSERT INTO mutation_info (mutation_id, gene_id, mutation_description) VALUES (1, 1, 'Mutation description');</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE sequence_info (
